<script>\\\\r\\\\n        let chats = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(\\\'geminiHubChats\\\')) || [];\\\\r\\\\n        let activeTag = null;\\\\r\\\\n        let currentEditingTasks = [];\\\\r\\\\n        let currentEditingTags = []; \\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function init() { \\\\r\\\\n            updateAutoTags(); \\\\r\\\\n            renderChats(); \\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        // --- MANUAL CONTROLS ---\\\\r\\\\n        function openManual() { document.getElementById(\\\'manualModal\\\').classList.remove(\\\'hidden\\\'); }\\\\r\\\\n        function closeManual() {  if (e.target === document.getElementById(\\\'manualModal\\\')) closeManual();\\\\r\\\\n        });\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function updateAutoTags() {\\\\r\\\\n            let changed = false;\\\\r\\\\n            chats.forEach(chat => {\\\\r\\\\n                if (!chat.tags) chat.tags = [];\\\\r\\\\n                const hasPending = chat.tasks && chat.tasks.some(t => !t.done);\\\\r\\\\n                // Use English tag \\\\"Pending\\\\"\\\\r\\\\n                const pendingIndex = chat.tags.findIndex(t => t.toLowerCase() === \\\'pending\\\' || t.toLowerCase() === \\\'pendientes\\\');\\\\r\\\\n                \\\\r\\\\n                if (hasPending && pendingIndex === -1) { \\\\r\\\\n                    chat.tags.push(\\\'Pending\\\'); \\\\r\\\\n                    changed = true; \\\\r\\\\n                } else if (!hasPending && pendingIndex !== -1) { \\\\r\\\\n                    chat.tags.splice(pendingIndex, 1); \\\\r\\\\n                    changed = true; \\\\r\\\\n                }\\\\r\\\\n            });\\\\r\\\\n            if (changed) saveData();\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        // --- HEADER STATS ---\\\\r\\\\n        function updateHeaderStats(counts) {\\\\r\\\\n            const total = chats.length;\\\\r\\\\n            const statsContainer = document.getElementById(\\\'header-stats\\\');\\\\r\\\\n   function linkify(text) {\\\\r\\\\n            if (!text) return \\\'\\\';\\\\r\\\\n            return text.replace(/(https?:\\\\\\\\/\\\\\\\\/[^\\\\\\\\s]+)/g, url => `<a href=\\\\"${url}\\\\" target=\\\\"_blank\\\\" class=\\\\"text-blue-600 hover:underline break-all relative z-10\\\\" onclick=\\\\"event.stopPropagation()\\\\">${url}</a>`);\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function renderTaskEditor() {\\\\r\\\\n            const list = document.getElementById(\\\'taskList\\\');\\\\r\\\\n            list.innerHTML = \\\'\\\';\\\\r\\\\n            if (currentEditingTasks.length === 0) {\\\\r\\\\n                list.innerHTML = \\\'<li class=\\\\"text-xs text-gray-400 italic text-center py-2\\\\">No pending tasks.</li>\\\';\\\\r\\\\n                return;\\\\r\\\\n            }\\\\r\\\\n            currentEditingTasks.forEach((task, index) => {\\\\r\\\\n                const li = document.createElement(\\\'li\\\');\\\\r\\\\n                li.className = \\\'flex items-center gap-2 bg-white p-2 rounded border border-gray-200 hover:border-indigo-300 transition-colors group\\\';\\\\r\\\\n                li.innerHTML = `<input document.getElementById(\\\'tag-suggestions\\\').classList.add(\\\'hidden\\\'); }\\\\r\\\\n        function removeEditingTag(index) { currentEditingTags.splice(index, 1); renderEditingTags(); !currentEditingTags.includes(tag) && (!val || tag.toLowerCase().includes(val)));\\\\r\\\\n            const box = document.getElementById(\\\'tag-suggestions\\\');\\\\r\\\\n            if e.stopPropagation(); addEditingTag(tag); input.focus(); }; box.appendChild(div);\\\\r\\\\n            });\\\\r\\\\n            box.classList.remove(\\\'hidden\\\');\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n        function closeSuggestions() { setTimeout(() => document.getElementById(\\\'tag-suggestions\\\').classList.add(\\\'hidden\\\'), 200); }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function drag(ev, id) { ev.dataTransfer.setData(\\\\"text/plain\\\\", id); setTimeout(() => ev.target.classList.add(\\\'dragging\\\'), 0); }\\\\r\\\\n        function dragEnd(ev) { ev.target.classList.remove(\\\'dragging\\\'); document.querySelectorAll(\\\'.drop-zone-active\\\').forEach(el => el.classList.remove(\\\'drop-zone-active\\\')); }\\\\r\\\\n        function allowDrop(ev) { ev.preventDefault(); ev.currentTarget.classList.add(\\\'drop-zone-active\\\'); }\\\\r\\\\n        function leaveDrop(ev) { ev.currentTarget.classList.remove(\\\'drop-zone-active\\\'); }\\\\r\\\\n        function drop(ev, newPriority) {\\\\r\\\\n            ev.preventDefault(); ev.currentTarget.classList.remove(\\\'drop-zone-active\\\');\\\\r\\\\n            const id = parseInt(ev.dataTransfer.getData(\\\\"text/plain\\\\"));\\\\r\\\\n            const chatIndex = chats.findIndex(c => c.id === id);\\\\r\\\\n            if (chatIndex > -1 && chats[chatIndex].priority !== newPriority) { chats[chatIndex].priority = newPriority; saveData(); renderChats(); }\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function saveData() { localStorage.setItem(\\\'geminiHubChats\\\', JSON.stringify(chats)); }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function handleFormSubmit(e) {\\\\r\\\\n            e.preventDefault();\\\\r\\\\n            const editId = document.getElementById(\\\'editId\\\').value;\\\\r\\\\n            const title = document.getElementById(\\\'inputTitle\\\').value;\\\\r\\\\n            let path = document.getElementById(\\\'inputPath\\\').value.trim();\\\\r\\\\n            const link = document.getElementById(\\\'inputLink\\\').value.trim();\\\\r\\\\n            const priority = document.querySelector(\\\'input[name=\\\\"priority\\\\"]:checked\\\').value;\\\\r\\\\n            const desc = document.getElementById(\\\'inputDesc\\\').value;\\\\r\\\\n            let tags = \\\\"Pending\\\\" (English) and legacy \\\\"Pendientes\\\\" (Spanish)\\\\r\\\\n            tags = tags.filter(t => t.toLowerCase() !== \\\'pending\\\' && t.toLowerCase() !== \\\'pendientes\\\');\\\\r\\\\n            if (pendingTasks > 0) tags.push(\\\'Pending\\\');\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n            if (path && !path.toLowerCase().endsWith(\\\'.html\\\') && !path.toLowerCase().endsWith(\\\'.htm\\\')) path += \\\'.html\\\';\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n            const chatData = { title, path, link, priority, desc, tags, tasks: currentEditingTasks };\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n            if (editId) {\\\\r\\\\n                const index = chats.findIndex(c => c.id == editId);\\\\r\\\\n                if (index !== -1) chats[index] = { ...chats[index], ...chatData };\\\\r\\\\n            } else {\\\\r\\\\n                chats.push({ id: Date.now(), ...chatData, date: new Date().toLocaleDateString() });\\\\r\\\\n            }\\\\r\\\\n            saveData();\\\\r\\\\n            closeModal();\\\\r\\\\n            renderChats();\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function deleteChat(id) {\\\\r\\\\n            if(confirm(\\\'Delete this item?\\\')) {\\\\r\\\\n                chats = chats.filter(c => c.id !== id);\\\\r\\\\n                saveData(); renderChats();\\\\r\\\\n            }\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function toggleFavorite(e, id) {\\\\r\\\\n            e.stopPropagation(); \\\\r\\\\n            const index = chats.findIndex(c => c.id === id);\\\\r\\\\n            if (index === -1) return;\\\\r\\\\n            let tags = chats[index].tags || [];\\\\r\\\\n            // Handle English and Legacy Spanish tags\\\\r\\\\n            if (tags.includes(\\\'favorites\\\') tags.push(\\\'Favorites\\\'); // Use English\\\\r\\\\n            }\\\\r\\\\n            chats[index].tags = tags;\\\\r\\\\n            saveData(); renderChats();\\\\r\\\\n        }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function setTagFilter(tag) { activeTag = (activeTag === tag) ? null : tag; renderChats(); }\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n        function renderTagFilters(allTags, pendingCount,            container.innerHTML = \\\'\\\';\\\\r\\\\n            statusContainer.innerHTML = \\\'\\\';\\\\r\\\\n\\\\r\\\\n            const allActive = activeTag === null;\\\\r\\\\n            const transition-all">Save</button>\n                </div>\n            </form>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <script>\n        // Global state\n        let knowledgeCards = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(\'helixCollectiveCards\')) || [];\n        let activeAgent = null;\n        let activeTag = null;\n        let currentEditingTasks = [];\n        let currentEditingTags = [];\n        let connectedAgents = [];\n        let collectiveIntelligence = 0.0;\n\n        // API endpoint\n        const API_BASE = window.location.hostname === \'localhost\' ? \n            \'http://localhost:8000\' : \'https://helix-collective-hub.up.railway.app\';\n\n        function init() {\n            loadAgents();\n            loadStats();\n            renderChats();\n            updateAutoTags();\n            startRealtimeUpdates();\n        }\n\n        async function loadAgents() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/agents`);\n                const data = await response.json();\n                connectedAgents = [...data.manus_instances, ...data.claude_instances];\n                \n                const container = document.getElementById(\'agent-filters\');\n                container.innerHTML = \'<button onclick="setAgentFilter(null)" class="px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold border bg-purple-600 text-white border-purple-600">All Agents</button>\';\n                \n                connectedAgents.forEach(agent => {\n                    const btn = document.createElement(\'button\');\n                    btn.className = \'px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-bold border bg-white text-gray-600 border-gray-300 hover:border-purple-300 hover:text-purple-600 hover:bg-purple-50\';\n                    btn.textContent = agent.code_name;\n                    btn.onclick = () => setAgentFilter(agent.code_name);\n                    container.appendChild(btn);\n                });\n                \n                document.getElementById(\'agent-status\').innerHTML = `\n                    <span class="flex items-center gap-2">\n                        <i class="ph-fill ph-users-three text-green-400"></i>\n                        ${connectedAgents.length} Agents Connected\n                    </span>\n                `;\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.log(\'Backend not available, using local mode\');\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function loadStats() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/dashboard/stats`);\n                const stats = await response.json();\n                \n                document.getElementById(\'header-stats\').innerHTML = `\n                    <span class="font-bold text-purple-200">Cards: ${stats.total_knowledge_cards}</span>\n                    <span class="mx-3 text-purple-500/50 text-lg">|</span>\n                    <span>Contributions: ${stats.total_agent_contributions}</span>\n                    <span class="mx-3 text-purple-500/50 text-lg">|</span>\n                    <span>CI Score: ${stats.collective_intelligence_growth.toFixed(2)}</span>\n                `;\n                \n                collectiveIntelligence = stats.collective_intelligence_growth;\n                document.getElementById(\'ci-score\').textContent = collectiveIntelligence.toFixed(2);\n            } catch (error) {\n                updateLocalStats();\n            }\n        }\n\n        function updateLocalStats() {\n            const total = knowledgeCards.length;\n            const avgUCF = knowledgeCards.reduce((sum, card) => sum + (card.ucf_score || 0), 0) / total || 0;\n            \n            document.getElementById(\'header-stats\').innerHTML = `\n                <span class="font-bold text-purple-200">Cards: ${total}</span>\n                <span class="mx-3 text-purple-500/50 text-lg">|</span>\n                <span>Local Mode</span>\n                <span class="mx-3 text-purple-500/50 text-lg">|</span>\n                <span>UCF: ${avgUCF.toFixed(2)}</span>\n            `;\n            \n            document.getElementById(\'ci-score\').textContent = avgUCF.toFixed(2);\n        }\n\n        function setAgentFilter(agent) {\n            activeAgent = activeAgent === agent ? null : agent;\n            renderChats();\n        }\n\n        function drag(ev, id) { \n            ev.dataTransfer.setData("text/plain", id); \n            setTimeout(() => ev.target.classList.add(\'dragging\'), 0); \n        }\n        \n        function dragEnd(ev) { \n            ev.target.classList.remove(\'dragging\'); \n            document.querySelectorAll(\'.drop-zone-active\').forEach(el => el.classList.remove(\'drop-zone-active\')); \n        }\n        \n        function allowDrop(ev) { \n            ev.preventDefault(); \n            ev.currentTarget.classList.add(\'drop-zone-active\'); \n        }\n        \n        function leaveDrop(ev) { \n            ev.currentTarget.classList.remove(\'drop-zone-active\'); \n        }\n        \n        function drop(ev, newPriority) {\n            ev.preventDefault(); \n            ev.currentTarget.classList.remove(\'drop-zone-active\'); \n            const id = parseInt(ev.dataTransfer.getData("text/plain")); \n            const cardIndex = knowledgeCards.findIndex(c => c.id === id); \n            if (cardIndex > -1 && knowledgeCards[cardIndex].priority !== newPriority) { \n                knowledgeCards[cardIndex].priority = newPriority; \n                saveData(); \n                renderChats(); \n            } \n        }\n\n        function saveData() { \n            localStorage.setItem(\'helixCollectiveCards\', JSON.stringify(knowledgeCards)); \n        }\n\n        function renderChats() {\n            const cols = { \n                idea: document.getElementById(\'col-idea\'), \n                pinned: document.getElementById(\'col-pinned\'), \n                important: document.getElementById(\'col-important\'), \n                reference: document.getElementById(\'col-reference\') \n            };\n            \n            const searchVal = document.getElementById(\'searchInput\').value.toLowerCase();\n            Object.values(cols).forEach(el => el.innerHTML = \'\'); \n            let counts = { idea: 0, pinned: 0, important: 0, reference: 0 }; \n\n            knowledgeCards.forEach(card => {\n                const matchesSearch = !searchVal || (card.title.toLowerCase().includes(searchVal) || (card.description && card.description.toLowerCase().includes(searchVal))); \n                if (matchesSearch) { \n                    if (activeAgent && card.agent_name !== activeAgent) return; \n                    if (!counts.hasOwnProperty(card.priority)) card.priority = \'reference\'; \n                    counts[card.priority]++; \n                    cols[card.priority].innerHTML += createCard(card); \n                } \n            });\n\n            Object.keys(counts).forEach(key => {\n                document.getElementById(`count-${key === \'pinned\' ? \'pin\' : key === \'important\' ? \'imp\' : key === \'reference\' ? \'ref\' : key}`).innerText = counts[key];\n            });\n        }\n\n        function createCard(card) {\n            const hasDescription = card.description && card.description.length > 0;\n            const mainTitle = card.title;\n            \n            let agentBadge = \'\';\n            if (card.agent_name) {\n                agentBadge = `<div class="agent-badge">${card.agent_name}</div>`;\n            }\n            \n            let ucfBadge = \'\';\n            if (card.ucf_score && card.ucf_score > 0) {\n                ucfBadge = `<div class="ucf-score">${card.ucf_score.toFixed(1)}</div>`;\n            }\n            \n            let tagsHtml = \'\';\n            if (card.tags && card.tags.length > 0) { \n                tagsHtml = `<div class="flex flex-wrap gap-1 mt-2 mb-1">`; \n                card.tags.forEach(tag => { \n                    if (tag.toLowerCase() !== \'pending\') {\n                        tagsHtml += `<button onclick="setTagFilter(\'${tag}\')" class="px-1.5 py-0.5 text-[10px] rounded font-medium border bg-teal-50 text-teal-700 border-teal-100 hover:bg-teal-100 hover:border-teal-300 cursor-pointer">#${tag}</button>`; \n                    }\n                }); \n                tagsHtml += `</div>`; \n            }\n\n            let progressHtml = \'\';\n            if (card.tasks && card.tasks.length > 0) { \n                const total = card.tasks.length; \n                const done = card.tasks.filter(t => t.done).length; \n                const percent = Math.round((done / total) * 100); \n                const colorClass = percent === 100 ? \'bg-green-600\' : \'bg-green-400\'; \n                progressHtml = `<div class="mt-2 mb-1"><div class="flex justify-between text-[10px] mb-0.5 text-gray-500"><span>Tasks</span><span>${done}/${total} (${percent}%)</span></div><div class="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-1.5"><div class="${colorClass} h-1.5 rounded-full transition-all duration-500" style="width: ${percent}%"></div></div></div>`; \n            }\n\n            const descHtml = card.description ? `<p class="text-sm text-gray-500 line-clamp-2 mt-1">${card.description}</p>` : \'\'; \n\n            return ` \n                <div class="card-${card.priority} card-base card-hover p-4 rounded-lg shadow-sm border border-gray-100 relative group flex flex-col gap-1" draggable="true" ondragstart="drag(event, ${card.id})" ondragend="dragEnd(event)"> \n                    <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-1"> \n                        <div class="font-bold text-gray-800 text-lg leading-tight pr-2 block max-w-[75%]">${mainTitle}</div> \n
